##### `precision()`

Precision of number in radix 10.

The `BigInteger` class does not have a `precision()` method. Therefore, for this test, precision is determined with [`Numbers.precision(BigInteger)`][Numbers].

⡇⢀⠀⡀⠀⠀⠀⡀⣀⣀⡠⠔⠊⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠑⠒⠤⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸
